# Siberian Tiger
narrative_event = {
	id = ko.1
	desc = EVTDESC_KO_001
	picture = GFX_evt_white_tiger
	title = EVTTITLE_KO_001
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	only_playable = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	min_age = 16
	
	trigger = {
			has_landed_title = k_korea
	}
	
weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = slothful   
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = diligent  
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = trusting
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = patient
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = wroth
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = proud
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = humble
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 5
			trait = hunter
		}
		}

		
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_KO_001
		
		 character_event = { id = ko.031 }								
	}
		option = {
		name = EVTOPTB_KO_001
		custom_tooltip = { text = EVTOPTB_KO_001_TT }
		 character_event = { id = ko.080 days = 14 }								
	}
		option = {
		name = EVTOPTC_KO_001
		custom_tooltip = { text = EVTOPTC_KO_001_TT }	
				random_list = {
			10 = { add_trait = cruel }
			90 = { prestige = -10 }
			}
		}
		option = {
		name = EVTOPTD_KO_001
		trigger = { has_global_flag = tiger_killings }
		piety = 20
		prestige = 40
		clr_global_flag = tiger_kllings
		}		
	}

# Invite vassals to feast
character_event = {
	id = ko.200
	desc = EVTDESC_KO_075
	picture = GFX_evt_emissary

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_KO_075
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_character_modifier = holding_chuseok_feast
			}
			any_vassal = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { is_inaccessible_trigger = yes }
					prisoner = no
					war = no
					in_command = no
					NOT = { trait = incapable }
					age = 16
				}
				letter_event = {
					id = ko.201
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_married = yes
			}
			hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = ko.205 } }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_married = no
				has_lover = yes
			}
			hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = ko.206 } }
		}
		hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = ko.208 days = 12 } }
	}
}

# Vassal receives invitation - Chuseok
letter_event = {
	id = ko.201
	desc = EVTDESC_KO_076
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = { NOT = { is_inaccessible_trigger = yes } }
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_KO_076 #Travel to the feast
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 2
			modifier = {
				factor = 5
				has_focus = focus_carousing
			}
			modifier  = {
				factor = 0.1
				is_inaccessible_trigger = yes
			}
			modifier  = {
				factor = 2
				opinion = { who = from value = -30 }
			}
			modifier  = {
				factor = 5
				opinion = { who = from value = -15 }
			}
			modifier  = {
				factor = 5
				opinion = { who = from value = 0 }
			}
		}
		character_event = { id = ko.202 days = 12 } 
		 character_event = { id = ko.222 days = 42 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_married = yes
			}
			hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = ko.205 } }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_married = no
				has_lover = yes
			}
			hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = ko.206 } }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB_KO_076 #Refuse invitation
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier  = {
				factor = 0
				opinion = { who = from value = 25 } 
				NOT = { is_inaccessible_trigger = yes }
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			letter_event = {
				id = ko.204
				days = 3
			}
		}
	}
}

# Feast begins
character_event = {
	id = ko.208
	desc = EVTDESC_KO_081
	picture = GFX_evt_chuseok

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_KO_081
		hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = ko.229 days = 25 } } # Religious ceremony
		hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = ko.209 days = 30 } } # End feast
		hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = ko.222 days = 31 } } # Clearing all flags and modifiers after feast
		set_character_flag = chuseok_feast_begun
		hidden_tooltip = {
			random_list = {
				15 = { character_event = { id = ko.214 days = 10 random = 6 } } # Snake charmer
				15 = { character_event = { id = ko.232 days = 10 random = 6 } } # Songpyeon A
				15 = { character_event = { id = ko.234 days = 10 random = 6 } } # Songpyeon B
				15 = { character_event = { id = ko.236 days = 10 random = 6 } } # Hangwa
				15 = { character_event = { id = ko.223 days = 10 random = 6 } } # Magician
				15 = { character_event = { id = ko.228 days = 10 random = 6 } } # Monkeys
				15 = { character_event = { id = ko.243 days = 10 random = 6 } } # Harvest Moon
				
				100 = {} # No random event
			}
					random_list = {
				15 = { character_event = { id = ko.291 days = 20 random = 6 } } # Dancers
				15 = { modifier = { factor = 0 has_children = no } character_event = { id = ko.290 days = 10 random = 6 } } # Waterbirds
				15 = { modifier = { factor = 0.1 trait = slothful }
					   modifier = { factor = 0.5 trait = paranoid }
					   modifier = { factor = 2 trait = diligent }
					   modifier = { factor = 2 trait = proud }
					   modifier = { factor = 2 trait = humble }
					   modifier = { factor = 2 trait = gregarious }
					   modifier = { factor = 0.1 trait = cynical } character_event = { id = ko.237 days = 20 random = 6 } } # Tending Graves
				15 = { modifier = { factor = 2 trait = gregarious } modifier = { factor = 2 trait = drunkard } modifier = { factor = 0.1 trait = temperate } character_event = { id = ko.238 days = 15 random = 6 } } # Give drinks to kids
				15 = { character_event = { id = ko.239 days = 15 random = 6 } } # Broken Contest
				15 = { character_event = { id = ko.254 days = 12 random = 6 } } # Ice
				2 = { modifier = { factor = 0 NOT = { year = 1066 } } modifier = { factor = 0 job_marshal = { is_alive = no } } character_event = { id = ko.299 days = 3 random = 6 } } # Marshal story 3
				2 = { modifier = { factor = 0 job_marshal = { is_alive = no } } character_event = { id = ko.298 days = 2 random = 6 } } # Marshal story 2 
				2 = { modifier = { factor = 0 job_marshal = { is_alive = no } } character_event = { id = ko.297 days = 4 random = 6 } } # Marshal story 1
				10 = { modifier = { factor = 0 is_female = no } character_event = { id = ko.804 days = 5 random = 6 } } # Hwajeonnori
				
			}	
		}
		any_courtier = {
			limit = {
				is_adult = yes
				is_ruler = no
				NOT = { trait = incapable }
			}
			set_character_flag = attending_chuseok_feast
			hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = ko.222 days = 31 } } # Clearing all flags and modifiers after feast
		}
	}
}

# Vassal arrives at feast
character_event = {
	id = ko.202

	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		set_character_flag = attending_chuseok_feast
		random_list = { # Choose random event
			1 = { character_event = { id = ko.232 days = 10 random = 5 } } # Songpyeon A
			2 = { character_event = { id = ko.234 days = 10 random = 5 } } # Songpyeon B
			1 = { character_event = { id = ko.236 days = 10 random = 5 } } # Hangwa
			10 = { character_event = { id = ko.223 days = 10 random = 5 } } # Magician
			10 = { character_event = { id = ko.228 days = 10 random = 5 } } # Birds
			2 = {  character_event = { id = ko.238 days = 15 random = 6 } } # Give drinks to kids
			2 = { character_event = { id = ko.243 days = 11 random = 6 } } # Harvest Moon
			120 = {} # No random event
		}
	}
}

# Feast ends
character_event = {
	id = ko.209

	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_character_flag = bad_chuseok
			}
			character_event = { id = ko.210 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_character_flag = bad_chuseok }
			}
			character_event = { id = ko.211 }
		}
		any_vassal = {
			limit = {
				has_character_flag = attending_chuseok_feast
				ROOT = { is_liege_of = THIS }
				has_character_flag = bad_chuseok
			}
			character_event = { id = ko.212 }
		}
		any_vassal = {
			limit = {
				has_character_flag = attending_chuseok_feast
				ROOT = { is_liege_of = THIS }
				NOT = { has_character_flag = bad_chuseok }
			}
			character_event = { id = ko.213 }
		}
	}
}

	id = ko.217
	desc = EVTDESC_KO_089
	picture = GFX_evt_kfeast

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_KO_089
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { trait = stressed }
				NOT = { trait = craven }
			}
			add_trait = stressed
			set_character_flag = bad_chuseok
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					trait = stressed
					trait = craven
				}
			}
			hidden_tooltip = {
				random_list = {
					10 = {
						if = {
							limit = {
								NOT = {
									has_dlc = "Reapers"
								}
							}
							add_trait = ill
						}
						if = {
							limit = {
								has_dlc = "Reapers"
							}
							add_symptom_effect = yes
						}
						set_character_flag = bad_chuseok
						character_event = { id = 38290 } # Notify
					}
					10 = {
						add_trait = stutter
						set_character_flag = bad_chuseok
						character_event = { id = 38253 } # Notify
					}
					10 = {
						add_trait = depressed
						set_character_flag = bad_chuseok
						character_event = { id = 38288 } # Notify
					}
					10 = {
						add_trait = lunatic
						set_character_flag = bad_chuseok
						character_event = { id = 38304 } # Notify
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

			trait = cruel
			NOT = { trait = impaler }
		}
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = entertaining_entertainment
			days = 730
		}
		clr_character_flag = bad_chuseok
	}
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTD_KO_097
		tooltip_info = inbred
		trigger = {
			trait = inbred
			NOT = { trait = imbecile }
		}
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = good_times
			days = 730
		}
		clr_character_flag = bad_chuseok
	}
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTD_KO_097
		tooltip_info = imbecile
		trigger = {
			trait = imbecile
			NOT = { trait = inbred }
		}
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = good_times
			days = 730
		}
		clr_character_flag = bad_chuseok
	}
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTE_KO_097
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				trait = stressed
				trait = depressed
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { trait = stressed }
			remove_trait = stressed
		}
		if = {
			limit = { trait = depressed }
			remove_trait = depressed
		}
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = good_times
			days = 730
		}
		clr_character_flag = bad_chuseok
	}
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTF_KO_097

				trait = craven
				trait = paranoid
			}
		}
		add_trait = stressed
		set_character_flag = bad_chuseok
	}

  trait = martial_cleric
  trait = scholarly_theologian
  trait = mastermind_theologian

  is_female = yes
  trait = possessed
  trait = lunatic
  
} } }

		days = 1

			factor = 2
			trait = slothful

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = diligent  
		}

			factor = 0.5
			trait = trusting
		}

		}

	war = no

		in_command = no
		any_vassal = {
			war = no
			prisoner = no
			age = 20
			reverse_opinion = { who = ROOT value = 20 }
		}
	}

		set_character_flag = dano_event_happened
	}

		days = 198

			factor = 0.33
			NOT = { has_character_flag = dano_event_happened }
		}	
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			has_character_flag = dano_event_happened
		}

# Wa pirates spot
character_event = {
	id = ko.620
	desc = EVTDESC_KO_620
	picture = GFX_evt_underwater_king

	is_triggered_only = yes

			option = {
			name = EVTOPTA_KO_620
					if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { martial = 15 }
			}
		hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = ko.622 } }	
		}
					if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { martial = 10 }
			}
		hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = ko.621 } }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { martial = 5 }
			}
			hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = ko.623 } }
		}
	}
				option = {
			name = EVTOPTB_KO_620
				random_list = {
				15 = { character_event = { id = ko.627 } }
				15 = { character_event = { id = ko.628 } }
				15 = { character_event = { id = ko.629 } }
				15 = { character_event = { id = ko.630 } }
				20 = { character_event = { id = ko.631 } }
				20 = { character_event = { id = ko.632 } }
				}
				}
					option = {
			name = EVTOPTC_KO_620
					if = {
			limit = {
				is_alive = yes
				prestige = 4000
			}
			hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = ko.634 } }
		}
							if = {
			limit = { is_alive = yes }
			hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = ko.633 } }
		}
	}
}

# Inconclusive Failure
character_event = {
	id = ko.625
	desc = EVTDESC_KO_625
	picture = GFX_evt_sailing_dark

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_global_flag = aliens_from_outer_space }
			}
				if = {
					limit = {
							e_japan = {
								holder_scope = {
									always = yes
								}
							}
					}
				 imprison = FROM
				}
			}
		}	
	
			option = {
			name = EVTOPTA_KO_625
			character_event = { id = ko.626 }
	}
}

character_event = {
	id = ko.720

	picture = GFX_evt_war_planning
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_war
	is_triggered_only = yes
	desc = EVTDESC_KO_347
	only_playable = yes
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no

	
	trigger = {
		has_focus = focus_war
		has_character_flag = martial_hagseng
		can_have_more_leadership_traits = yes
		OR = {
			NOT = { trait = cavalry_leader }
			NOT = { has_character_flag = strat_gosu }
			AND = {
				NOT = { trait = holy_warrior }
				trait = zealous
			}
		}
	}
	
weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.25
			trait = misguided_warrior
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			trait = tough_soldier
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = skilled_tactician
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 3.0
			trait = brilliant_strategist
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.1
			NOT = { martial = 5 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			NOT = { martial = 8 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			NOT = { martial = 12 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			has_character_modifier = adept_of_strategy
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 3.0
			trait = strategist
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.25
			leader_traits = 1
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_KO_347 # More developed
	character_event = { id = ko.721 }
	}
		option = {
		name = EVTOPTB_KO_347 # Horse archers
	character_event = { id = ko.722 }
	}
		option = {
		name = EVTOPTC_KO_347 # Plague
	character_event = { id = ko.723 }
	}
	
}

		NOT = { religion_group = muslim }
		NOT = { religion = tengri_pagan }
		NOT = { religion = tengri_pagan_reformed }		
	}

		days = 1

			factor = 2
			trait = slothful

			factor = 0.5

		}

			factor = 0.5

		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 3
			trait = wroth
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5

		}

		} }

	}

									prisoner = no
									NOT = { trait = incapable }

					}

# Your dynasty is false! 2

character_event = {
	id = ko.301
	desc = EVTDESC_KO_321.1
	picture = GFX_evt_judged_by_ruler
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	only_playable = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
	random_courtier = {
	limit = { OR = { is_foe = ROOT
					has_focus = focus_intrigue
					learning = 12
					intrigue = 10	} }
	save_event_target_as = go_dynasty_liar
		}
	random_courtier = {
	limit = { OR = { is_foe = ROOT
					has_focus = focus_intrigue
					learning = 12
					intrigue = 10
					diplomacy = 10	} }
	save_event_target_as = go_dynasty_liartwo
		}
	}	
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_KO_321.1
		any_vassal = {
			opinion = {
				modifier = opinion_tyrant
				who = ROOT
				years = 15
			}	
		}	
		event_target:go_dynasty_liar  = {
			death = {
			death_reason = death_execution_beheading }
			}
		event_target:go_dynasty_liartwo  = {
			death = {
			death_reason = death_execution_beheading }
			}
		}
			
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB_KO_321.1
				any_vassal = { limit = { is_friend = event_target:go_dynasty_liar
										is_close_relative = event_target:go_dynasty_liar } 
			opinion = {
				modifier = opinion_tyrant
				who = ROOT
				years = 5
			}	
		}
		event_target:go_dynasty_liar  = {
			imprison = ROOT
			}
		event_target:go_dynasty_liartwo  = {
			imprison = ROOT
			}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTC_KO_321.1
		trigger = { trait = cynical } 
						any_vassal = {
				limit = { NOT = { trait = cynical } }
			opinion = {
				modifier = opinion_honorable
				who = ROOT
				years = 5
			}	
		}
						any_courtier = {
				limit = { is_adult = no }
			opinion = {
				modifier = opinion_honorable
				who = ROOT
				years = 5
			}	
		}		
	}
		option = {
		name = EVTOPTD_KO_321.1
		tooltip_info = just
		trigger = { trait = just }
	prestige = 50	
	}
}
